### Project Structure
```
ftech_xs/
├── 计划书.md
├── 版本变更.md
├── config.json                  # Configuration file
├── download_novel.py            # Main download script
├── build_epub.py                # EPUB generation script
├── requirements.txt             # Python dependencies
├── <小说书名>/                  # e.g., 召唤圣剑/
│   ├── progress.json            # Download progress (for resume)
│   ├── chapters/                # Individual chapter files
│   │   ├── 0001.txt
│   │   ├── 0002.txt
│   │   └── ...
│   └── <小说书名>.epub          # Final EPUB output
└── utils/
    ├── __init__.py
    ├── scraper.py               # Web scraping utilities
    └── epub_builder.py          # EPUB building utilities
```

```
ftech_xs/

```

### 模块划分

| 模块 | 文件 | 职责 |
|------|------|------|
| 链接提取 | `download_novel.py` | 从章节目录页解析所有章节URL和标题 |
| 章节下载 | `download_novel.py` | 逐个下载章节HTML，含限速/重试/断点续传 |
| EPUB生成 | `build_epub.py` | 读取下载的章节文件，生成带目录的EPUB |

### 反爬对策
- `requests.Session()` 保持 Cookie
- 伪装 Chrome User-Agent + 完整请求头
- 每章间随机延迟 3-8 秒
- 空内容检测 → 等待 30-60s + 指数退避重试（最多5次）
- 断点续传：每下载一章立即保存进度

### EPUB 方案
- 使用 `ebooklib` 库生成标准 EPUB3
- 自动生成 NCX + nav.xhtml 目录
- 嵌入元数据（书名、作者）

# 📋 计划书.md (草案)

## 一、项目概述

| 项目 | 说明 |
|------|------|
| 项目名称 | ftech_xs - 小说下载与EPUB生成工具 |
| 目标网站 | `https://xn--1jqx9a.als1004.space` (爱丽丝书屋) |
| 首部目标小说 | 《召唤圣剑》(加料 校对版), ID=32157, Source=33719 |
| Python运行时 | `py -3` (Python 3.13.5) |
| 包管理 | `py -3 -m pip install` |

## 二、技术栈

| 组件 | 库 | 版本 | 用途 |
|------|-----|------|------|
| HTTP请求 | `requests` | 2.34.0 (已安装) | Session管理, 请求/重试 |
| HTML解析 | `beautifulsoup4` | 需安装 | 解析章节列表和内容 |
| XML解析 | `lxml` | 需安装 | BeautifulSoup后端, 加速解析 |
| EPUB生成 | `ebooklib` | 需安装 | EPUB结构构建, 目录生成 |
| JSON处理 | `json` (内置) | - | 配置文件/进度文件读写 |
| 路径处理 | `pathlib` (内置) | - | 跨平台路径 |
| 正则表达式 | `re` (内置) | - | HTML内容清洗 |
| 时间控制 | `time`, `random` (内置) | - | 延迟控制 |

## 三、目录结构

```
ftech_xs/
├── 计划书.md                      # 本文件，项目设计文档
├── 版本变更.md                     # 版本变更记录
├── requirements.txt               # Python依赖清单
├── config.json                    # 全局配置文件
├── download_novel.py              # 章节下载脚本
├── build_epub.py                  # EPUB生成脚本
└── <小说书名>/                    # 按书名动态创建，如：召唤圣剑/
    ├── config.json                # 该小说的配置（书籍ID等）
    ├── progress.json              # 下载进度文件，用于断点续传
    ├── chapters/                  # 下载的章节文件
    │   ├── 0001_第一章_新的旅程.html
    │   ├── 0002_第二章_圣剑套牌.html
    │   └── ...
    └── <小说书名>.epub            # 最终EPUB输出文件
```

## 四、配置文件设计

### 4.1 全局配置 `ftech_xs/config.json`

```json
{
    "base_url": "https://xn--1jqx9a.als1004.space",
    "request_delay": {
        "min": 3,
        "max": 8
    },
    "retry": {
        "max_attempts": 5,
        "backoff_base": 30,
        "backoff_multiplier": 2
    },
    "headers": {
        "User-Agent": "Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36...",
        "Accept": "text/html,application/xhtml+xml,application/xml;q=0.9,*/*;q=0.8",
        "Accept-Language": "zh-CN,zh;q=0.9,en;q=0.8",
        "Accept-Encoding": "gzip, deflate",
        "Connection": "keep-alive"
    }
}
```

### 4.2 小说配置 `ftech_xs/<书名>/config.json`

```json
{
    "book_name": "召唤圣剑",
    "book_id": 32157,
    "source_id": 33719,
    "author": "西贝猫",
    "chapters_url": "/other/chapters/id/32157.html"
}
```

## 五、模块设计

### 5.1 `download_novel.py` — 章节下载器

#### 程序入口
读取 `<书名>/config.json` 中的小说信息，从章节目录页提取所有章节链接，逐章下载并保存。

#### 5.1.1 链接提取 (`extract_chapters`)
```
输入: config (小说配置字典)
输出: chapters[] (章节列表，每项含 {index, title, url, hash})

流程:
1. GET {base_url}{chapters_url} → 获取章节目录页 HTML
2. BeautifulSoup 解析 <ul class="mulu_list"> 下的所有 <li><a>
3. 提取 href (/book/33719/<hash>.html) 和章节标题
4. 过滤掉非小说章节链接（第一部 黄昏篇 等卷标）
5. 返回有序章节列表
```

#### 5.1.2 章节下载 (`download_chapter`)
```
输入: session, chapter_url, chapter_info
输出: (success, html_content)

流程:
1. 构建完整 URL: {base_url}/book/{source_id}/{hash}.html
2. 设置 Referer 为章节目录页
3. GET 请求 → 检查状态码 200
4. 提取 <div class="read-content j_readContent user_ad_content"> 内的 HTML
5. 判空检测: 若 inner_html 为空或仅含空白 → 视为空内容
6. 返回结果
```

#### 5.1.3 AJAX备选下载 (`download_chapter_ajax`)
```
输入: session, chapter_info
输出: (success, html_content)

当 HTML 页面下载返回空内容时自动切换到此方式。

流程:
1. GET {base_url}/home/chapter/info?id={source_id}&key={hash}
2. 设置 Referer 和 X-Requested-With 等 AJAX 头
3. 解析 JSON 响应: resp['data']['chapter']['content']
4. 若 code != 1 或 content 为空 → 失败
5. 返回 HTML 内容
```

#### 5.1.4 空内容重试循环
```
输入: chapter (章节信息), session
输出: html_content

伪代码:
for attempt in 1..max_attempts:
    success, content = download_chapter(session, chapter.url, chapter)
    if not success:
        success, content = download_chapter_ajax(session, chapter)   # 备选
    if success:
        save_chapter(content)                                        # 保存成功
        return
    else:
        wait_time = backoff_base * (backoff_multiplier ** (attempt-1))
        log(f"第{chapter.index}章获取空内容, 等待{wait_time}秒后重试({attempt}/{max_attempts})")
        sleep(wait_time)

log(f"第{chapter.index}章下载失败, 已跳过")
save_progress(failed)                                               # 标记失败
```

#### 5.1.5 断点续传
```
流程:
1. 加载 progress.json:
   { "total": 679, "downloaded": [], "failed": [], "last_index": 0 }
2. 遍历章节列表，跳过已下载的 (index in downloaded)
3. 从 last_index 继续
4. 每下载一章:
   a. 保存 chapter_XXXX.html 到 chapters/ 目录
   b. 更新 progress.json (追加到 downloaded 数组, 更新 last_index)
5. 全部完成后标记 status: "complete"
```

#### 5.1.6 主流程控制
```
main(novel_name):
  1. 读取 config.json + <novel_name>/config.json
  2. 创建 Session + 初始化 headers
  3. extract_chapters(config) → 章节列表
  4. 加载/创建 progress.json
  5. for each chapter not in downloaded:
       sleep(random(min_delay, max_delay))
       download_with_retry(chapter, session)
  6. 打印下载统计: 成功X/总数, 失败Y
```

### 5.2 `build_epub.py` — EPUB生成器

#### 程序入口
读取 `<书名>/chapters/` 下的所有章节 HTML 文件和小说配置，生成一个带目录的 EPUB 文件。

#### 5.2.1 章节文件读取
```
1. 扫描 chapters/ 目录, 按文件名排序 (0001, 0002, ...)
2. 读取每个 HTML 文件的完整内容
3. 解析章节标题 (从文件名提取)
```

#### 5.2.2 EPUB 构建流程
```
1. 创建 epub.EpubBook() 对象
2. 设置元数据:
   - title: {书名}
   - creator: {作者}
   - language: 'zh-CN'
3. 设置 spine (linear='yes')
4. 为每个章节:
   a. 创建 EpubHtml 对象 (chapter_0001.xhtml)
   b. 设置标题为章节名
   c. 将 HTML 内容包裹在 <html><body> 中
   d. 添加 CSS: p { text-indent: 2em; line-height: 1.8; margin: 0.5em 0; }
   e. 加入 book 和 spine
5. 构建目录 (Table of Contents):
   - 使用 book.toc 添加 Section/SubSection
6. 添加默认 NCX 和 Nav 文件:
   - book.add_item(epub.EpubNcx())
   - book.add_item(epub.EpubNav())
7. 写入文件: epub.write_epub(<小说书名>/<小说书名>.epub, book, {})
```

## 六、进度文件格式 (progress.json)

```json
{
    "total": 679,
    "downloaded": [0, 1, 2, 3, 4],
    "failed": [],
    "last_index": 4,
    "status": "in_progress"
}
```

## 七、错误处理

| 错误类型 | 处理方式 |
|----------|----------|
| 网络超时 (30s) | 重试（计入attempt），每次翻倍等待 |
| HTTP 非200 | 重试，同上 |
| 空内容 | HTML→AJAX切换 → 重试 → 标记失败 |
| JSON解析失败 | 重试 → 标记失败 |
| config.json 不存在 | 打印错误并退出 |
| chapters 目录不存在 | 自动创建 |
| EPUB写入失败 | 打印错误并退出 |

## 八、依赖清单 (requirements.txt)

```
requests>=2.34.0
beautifulsoup4>=4.12.0
lxml>=5.0.0
ebooklib>=0.18
```

## 九、运行方式

```powershell
# 安装依赖
py -3 -m pip install -r requirements.txt

# 下载小说章节（需先在 ftech_xs/<书名>/ 下创建 config.json）
py -3 download_novel.py 召唤圣剑

# 生成 EPUB（需要在下载完成后）
py -3 build_epub.py 召唤圣剑
```

## Assistant (Plan · DeepSeek V4 Pro · 76.3s)

_Thinking:_

The user has two modification requests:

1. **Make it easy to support other URLs/books** - The current design has a per-book config.json, which already supports this, but I should make it clearer and more generic. Instead of requiring a config.json per book, maybe the user can just specify a URL and the script auto-detects everything.

2. **Change delay to 15-30 seconds** - Simple config change.

Let me update the plan to address these:

1. For multi-book support, the script should:
   - Accept a URL or book ID as parameter
   - Auto-detect the chapter listing URL pattern
   - Auto-extract book name, author, source_id from the site
   - Still support config.json for manual overrides
   - The config.json per book should be optional - if it doesn't exist, the script can auto-detect from the chapter listing URL

Actually, let me think about this more carefully. The user wants convenience for adding new books. Options:

**Option A**: Command-line URL-based
```bash
py -3 download_novel.py "https://xn--1jqx9a.als1004.space/other/chapters/id/32157.html"
```
The script auto-extracts book_id, source_id, book name from the page.

**Option B**: config.json with minimal fields
```json
{
    "chapters_url": "https://xn--1jqx9a.als1004.space/other/chapters/id/32157.html"
}
```
Everything else auto-detected.

**Option C**: Both - accept URL as argument OR use config.json if no argument given.

I think Option C is the best: CLI argument for quick use, config.json for repeated use. The script auto-detects everything from the chapters page.

Let me update the plan document accordingly.

Also need to update:
- Delay: 15-30 seconds
- Make URL/book discovery more explicit in the plan

Let me revise the relevant sections.

好建议。我来更新计划书应对这两点：

1. **多书支持**：将入口改为直接传入章节列表URL，脚本自动从页面提取书名、作者、book_id、source_id 等所有信息，不再需要手动编写 per-book config.json
2. **延迟调整**：15-30秒

以下是更新后的完整计划书：

---

# 📋 计划书.md (v1.0)

## 一、项目概述

| 项目 | 说明 |
|------|------|
| 项目名称 | ftech_xs - 爱丽丝书屋小说下载与EPUB生成工具 |
| 目标网站 | `https://xn--1jqx9a.als1004.space` |
| 运行环境 | Python 3.13.5, 命令: `py -3` |
| 包管理 | `py -3 -m pip install -r requirements.txt` |

**设计原则**: 只需提供一个章节列表URL，脚本自动完成一切——提取书名、作者、章节链接、下载、生成EPUB。

## 二、技术栈

| 库 | 用途 |
|----|------|
| `requests` (已安装 2.34.0) | HTTP Session 管理、请求、重试 |
| `beautifulsoup4` | HTML 解析（章节列表、章节内容） |
| `lxml` | HTML/XML 解析后端加速 |
| `ebooklib` | EPUB 构建、目录生成 |
| `json`, `pathlib`, `re`, `time`, `random`, `sys` | 标准库 |

## 三、目录结构

```
ftech_xs/
├── 计划书.md
├── 版本变更.md
├── requirements.txt
├── config.json                    # 全局配置（延迟、重试、请求头）
├── download_novel.py              # 章节下载脚本
├── build_epub.py                  # EPUB生成脚本
└── <小说书名>/                    # 自动根据书名创建
    ├── progress.json              # 下载进度（断点续传）
    ├── chapters/                  # 章节HTML文件
    │   ├── 0001_第一章_新的旅程.html
    │   └── ...
    └── <小说书名>.epub            # 最终EPUB
```

## 四、配置文件设计

### 4.1 全局配置 `ftech_xs/config.json`

```json
{
    "request_delay": {
        "min": 15,
        "max": 30
    },
    "retry": {
        "max_attempts": 5,
        "backoff_base": 30,
        "backoff_multiplier": 2
    },
    "headers": {
        "User-Agent": "Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/125.0.0.0 Safari/537.36",
        "Accept": "text/html,application/xhtml+xml,application/xml;q=0.9,image/avif,image/webp,*/*;q=0.8",
        "Accept-Language": "zh-CN,zh;q=0.9,en;q=0.8",
        "Accept-Encoding": "gzip, deflate",
        "Connection": "keep-alive",
        "Cache-Control": "no-cache"
    }
}
```

**不需要** 每本书单独建 config.json。小说名、作者、ID 等信息全部从章节列表页面自动提取。

## 五、模块设计

### 5.1 `download_novel.py` — 章节下载器

#### 用法

```powershell
# 方式一：传入完整URL
py -3 download_novel.py "https://xn--1jqx9a.als1004.space/other/chapters/id/32157.html"

# 方式二：仅传入ID（自动拼接URL）
py -3 download_novel.py 32157
```

#### 5.1.1 主流程

```
main(chapters_url):
  1. 加载全局 config.json
  2. 创建 requests.Session()，设置 headers
  3. fetch_book_info(session, chapters_url)
     → {book_name, author, book_id, source_id, chapters[]}
  4. 创建 <book_name>/ 和 <book_name>/chapters/ 目录
  5. 加载/创建 <book_name>/progress.json
  6. for each chapter not in progress.downloaded:
       sleep(random(15, 30))
       download_with_retry(session, chapter)
       save_chapter_to_file(chapter)
       update_progress()
  7. 打印统计: 成功 X/总数, 失败 Y
```

#### 5.1.2 书籍信息提取 (`fetch_book_info`)

```
输入: session, chapters_url
输出: book_info 字典

从章节列表页提取:
  - 书名: <div class="mu_h1"><h1> 的文本内容（去掉"《》"）
  - 作者: <span>作者：<a> 的文本
  - book_id: 从 chapters_url 正则提取 /id/(\d+) 
  - source_id: 从章节链接正则提取 /book/(\d+)/
  - chapters: 从 <ul class="mulu_list"> 所有 <li><a> 提取
    → 每项: {index, title, url, hash}
    → 过滤卷标链接（如"第一部 黄昏篇"）：标题不含"第.*章"且长度很短
```

#### 5.1.3 下载章节 (`download_chapter`)

```
输入: session, base_url, source_id, chapter_hash, chapter_index
输出: (success, html_content)

方式A — HTML页面下载:
  url = f"{base_url}/book/{source_id}/{chapter_hash}.html"
  设置 Referer = 章节列表页URL
  GET → 200 → 解析 <div class="read-content j_readContent user_ad_content">
  提取该 div 的 inner HTML（所有<p>标签）

方式B — AJAX API 备选（方式A返回空时自动切换）:
  url = f"{base_url}/home/chapter/info"
  params = {id: source_id, key: chapter_hash}
  设置 X-Requested-With: XMLHttpRequest
  GET → JSON → resp['data']['chapter']['content']

判定空内容:
  inner_html 去除空白字符后长度为 0 → 视为空内容
```

#### 5.1.4 空内容重试

```
attempt ∈ [1, max_attempts]:
  success, content = download_chapter(method="html")
  if not success:
    success, content = download_chapter(method="ajax")
  if success:
    保存文件, 更新进度 → 成功返回
  wait = backoff_base × (backoff_multiplier ^ (attempt-1)) 秒
  等待后重试

仍未成功 → 标记 failed, 记录日志
```

#### 5.1.5 章节文件保存

```
文件名: {index:04d}_{stripped_title}.html
  示例: 0001_新的旅程.html
  标题清理: 去掉第X章前缀, 去掉非法文件名字符 (? * : " < > |)

文件内容: 直接写入从页面提取的 inner HTML（保留 <p> 标签结构）
```

#### 5.1.6 断点续传

```
progress.json 格式:
{
    "book_name": "召唤圣剑",
    "chapters_url": "https://...",
    "total": 679,
    "downloaded": [0, 1, 2],
    "failed": [],
    "last_index": 2,
    "status": "in_progress"
}
每次下载完一个章节立即更新文件。
再次运行脚本时，跳过 downloaded 中的章节。
```

### 5.2 `build_epub.py` — EPUB生成器

#### 用法

```powershell
py -3 build_epub.py 召唤圣剑
```

#### 5.2.1 主流程

```
main(novel_dir):
  1. 检查 novel_dir/chapters/ 存在
  2. 扫描 chapters/ 目录下所有 .html 文件，按文件名数字前缀排序
  3. 读取每个 HTML 文件内容
  4. 构建 EpubBook:
     a. 设置元数据 (书名、作者、语言=zh-CN)
     b. 添加默认 CSS:
        p { text-indent: 2em; line-height: 1.8; margin: 0.5em 0; }
     c. 为每个章节创建 EpubHtml:
        - 文件名: chapter_{index:04d}.xhtml
        - 标题: 章节名
        - 内容: <html><body>{chapter_html}</body></html>
     d. 构建目录 (TOC):
        按章节顺序添加 Section 到 book.toc
     e. 添加 EpubNcx + EpubNav
  5. epub.write_epub() → <novel_dir>/<书名>.epub
  6. 打印成功信息
```

## 六、运行流程总览

```
用户                              脚本
 │                                 │
 ├─ py -3 download_novel.py URL ──┤
 │                                 ├─ 加载 config.json
 │                                 ├─ GET 章节列表页 → 解析书名/作者/章节
 │                                 ├─ 创建目录结构
 │                                 ├─ 逐章下载 (延迟15-30s) ──→ chapters/*.html
 │                                 └─ 完成 ──→ "成功 679/679"
 │                                 │
 ├─ py -3 build_epub.py 书名 ─────┤
 │                                 ├─ 扫描 chapters/*.html
 │                                 ├─ 构建 EPUB（元数据+TOC+内容）
 │                                 └─ 完成 ──→ 书名.epub
```

## 七、错误处理

| 错误 | 处理 |
|------|------|
| config.json 缺失 | 使用内置默认值 |
| 章节列表页 GET 失败 | 重试3次，仍失败则退出 |
| 书名提取失败 | 用 URL 中的 ID 作为备选书名 |
| 章节 HTML 下载返回空 | 切换到 AJAX API → 重试 → 失败标记 |
| 网络超时 (30s) | 计入 attempt，退避重试 |
| HTTP 非200 | 同上 |
| chapters 目录下无文件 | build_epub 报错退出 |
| EPUB 写入失败 | 报错退出 |

## 八、依赖

```
# requirements.txt
requests>=2.34.0
beautifulsoup4>=4.12.0
lxml>=5.0.0
ebooklib>=0.18
```

Some links are "volume markers" like "第一部 黄昏篇" - these should be filtered out. Looking at the pattern:
- Volume markers: no number pattern, just a name
- Chapter links: all follow "第X章" or "第X百Y十Z章" pattern

Both use the same URL pattern. The simplest filter: skip items that don't match `第.*章` or are clearly volume titles.

- Extracting book_id from URL: `/other/chapters/id/(\d+).html`

- Getting chapter hash from each link: `/book/\d+/([a-f0-9]+).html`

For the AJAX API:
- URL: `/home/chapter/info?id={source_id}&key={hash}`
- Response: `{"code": 1, "data": {"chapter": {"content": "...", "title": "...", ...}}}`

- `book.add_author(author)`
- `book.set_language('zh-CN')`

    ...
}
```

So the AJAX API returns `data.chapter.content` which is already HTML (like `<p>...</p><p>...</p>`). This is the same format as what we'd extract from the HTML page. So both methods return the same kind of content.

Now let me write everything.

```html
<html xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">
<head><title>Chapter Title</title></head>
<body>
  <h2>Chapter Title</h2>
  {chapter_content}

download_novel.py 32157\n```\n\n#### 5.1.1 主流程\n\n```\nmain(chapters_url):\n  1. 加载全局 config.json\n  2. 创建 requests.Session()，设置 headers\n  3. fetch_book_info(session, chapters_url)\n     → {book_name, author, book_id, source_id, chapters[]}\n  4. 创建 <book_name>/ 和 <book_name>/chapters/ 目录\n  5. 加载/创建 <book_name>/progress.json\n  6. for each chapter not in progress.downloaded:\n       sleep(random(15, 30))\n       download_with_retry(session, chapter)\n       save_chapter_to_file(chapter)\n       update_progress()\n  7. 打印统计: 成功 X/总数, 失败 Y\n```\n\n#### 5.1.2 书籍信息提取 (`fetch_book_info`)\n\n```\n输入: session, chapters_url\n输出: book_info 字典\n\n从章节列表页提取:\n  - 书名: <div class=\"mu_h1\"><h1> 的文本内容（去掉\"《》\"）\n  - 作者: <span>作者：<a> 的文本\n  - book_id: 从 chapters_url 正则提取 /id/(\\d+)\n  - source_id: 从章节链接正则提取 /book/(\\d+)/\n  - chapters: 从 <ul class=\"mulu_list\"> 所有 <li><a> 提取\n    → 每项: {index, title, url, hash}\n    → 过滤卷标链接（如\"第一部 黄昏篇\"）：标题不含\"第.*章\"且长度很短\n```\n\n#### 5.1.3 下载章节 (`download_chapter`)\n\n```\n输入: session, base_url, source_id, chapter_hash, chapter_index\n输出: (success, html_content)\n\n方式A — HTML页面下载:\n  url = f\"{base_url}/book/{source_id}/{chapter_hash}.html\"\n  设置 Referer = 章节列表页URL\n  GET → 200 → 解析 <div class=\"read-content j_readContent user_ad_content\">\n  提取该 div 的 inner HTML（所有<p>标签）\n\n方式B — AJAX API 备选（方式A返回空时自动切换）:\n  url = f\"{base_url}/home/chapter/info\"\n  params = {id: source_id, key: chapter_hash}\n  设置 X-Requested-With: XMLHttpRequest\n  GET → JSON → resp['data']['chapter']['content']\n\n判定空内容:\n  inner_html 去除空白字符后长度为 0 → 视为空内容\n```\n\n#### 5.1.4 空内容重试\n\n```\nattempt ∈ [1, max_attempts]:\n  success, content = download_chapter(method=\"html\")\n  if not success:\n    success, content = download_chapter(method=\"ajax\")\n  if success:\n    保存文件, 更新进度 → 成功返回\n  wait = backoff_base × (backoff_multiplier ^ (attempt-1)) 秒\n  等待后重试\n\n仍未成功 → 标记 failed, 记录日志\n```\n\n#### 5.1.5 章节文件保存\n\n```\n文件名: {index:04d}_{stripped_title}.html\n  示例: 0001_新的旅程.html\n  标题清理: 去掉第X章前缀, 去掉非法文件名字符 (? * : \" < > |)\n\n文件内容: 直接写入从页面提取的 inner HTML（保留 <p> 标签结构）\n```\n\n#### 5.1.6 断点续传\n\n```\nprogress.json 格式:\n{\n    \"book_name\": \"召唤圣剑\",\n    \"chapters_url\": \"https://...\",\n    \"total\": 679,\n    \"downloaded\": [0, 1, 2],\n    \"failed\": [],\n    \"last_index\": 2,\n    \"status\": \"in_progress\"\n}\n每次下载完一个章节立即更新文件。\n再次运行脚本时，跳过 downloaded 中的章节。\n```\n\n### 5.2 `build_epub.py` — EPUB生成器\n\n#### 用法\n\n```powershell\npy -3 build_epub.py 召唤圣剑\n```\n\n#### 5.2.1 主流程\n\n```\nmain(novel_dir):\n  1. 检查 novel_dir/chapters/ 存在\n  2. 扫描 chapters/ 目录下所有 .html 文件，按文件名数字前缀排序\n  3. 读取每个 HTML 文件内容\n  4. 构建 EpubBook:\n     a. 设置元数据 (书名、作者、语言=zh-CN)\n     b. 添加默认 CSS:\n        p { text-indent: 2em; line-height: 1.8; margin: 0.5em 0; }\n     c. 为每个章节创建 EpubHtml:\n        - 文件名: chapter_{index:04d}.xhtml\n        - 标题: 章节名\n        - 内容: <html xmlns=\"...\"><body><h2>{title}</h2>{html_content}</body></html>\n     d. 构建目录 (TOC):\n        按章节顺序添加 Section 到 book.toc\n     e. 添加 EpubNcx + EpubNav\n  5. epub.write_epub() → <novel_dir>/<书名>.epub\n  6. 打印成功信息\n```\n\n## 六、运行流程总览\n\n```\n用户                              脚本\n │                                 │\n ├─ py -3 download_novel.py URL ──┤\n │                                 ├─ 加载 config.json\n │                                 ├─ GET 章节列表页 → 解析书名/作者/章节\n │                                 ├─ 创建目录结构\n │                                 ├─ 逐章下载 (延迟15-30s) ──→ chapters/*.html\n │                                 └─ 完成 ──→ \"成功 679/679\"\n │                                 │\n ├─ py -3 build_epub.py 书名 ─────┤\n │                                 ├─ 扫描 chapters/*.html\n │                                 ├─ 构建 EPUB（元数据+TOC+内容）\n │                                 └─ 完成 ──→ 书名.epub\n```\n\n## 七、错误处理\n\n| 错误 | 处理 |\n|------|------|\n| config.json 缺失 | 使用内置默认值 |\n| 章节列表页 GET 失败 | 重试3次，仍失败则退出 |\n| 书名提取失败 | 用 URL 中的 ID 作为备选书名 |\n| 章节 HTML 下载返回空 | 切换到 AJAX API → 重试 → 失败标记 |\n| 网络超时 (30s) | 计入 attempt，退避重试 |\n| HTTP 非200 | 同上 |\n| chapters 目录下无文件 | build_epub 报错退出 |\n| EPUB 写入失败 | 报错退出 |\n\n## 八、依赖\n\n```\nrequests>=2.34.0\nbeautifulsoup4>=4.12.0\nlxml>=5.0.0\nebooklib>=0.18\n```\n"
}
```

标签结构）\n```\n\n#### 5.1.6 断点续传\n\n```\nprogress.json 格式:\n{\n    \"book_name\": \"召唤圣剑\",\n    \"chapters_url\": \"https://...\",\n    \"total\": 679,\n    \"downloaded\": [0, 1, 2],\n    \"failed\": build_epub.py 召唤圣剑\n```\n\n#### 5.2.1 主流程\n\n```\nmain(novel_dir):\n  1. 检查 novel_dir/chapters/ 存在\n  2. 扫描 chapters/ 目录下所有 .html 文件，按文件名数字前缀排序\n  3. 读取每个 HTML 文件内容\n  4. 构建 EpubBook:\n     a. 设置元数据 (书名、作者、语言=zh-CN)\n     b. 添加默认 CSS\n     c. 为每个章节创建 EpubHtml\n     d. 构建目录 (TOC)\n     e. 添加 EpubNcx + EpubNav\n  5. epub.write_epub() → <novel_dir>/<书名>.epub\n  6. 打印成功信息\n```\n\n## 六、运行流程总览\n\n```\n用户                              脚本\n │                                 │\n ├─ py -3 download_novel.py URL ──┤\n │                                 ├─ 加载 config.json\n │ 中的 ID 作为备选书名 |\n| 章节 HTML 下载返回空 | 切换到 AJAX API → 重试 → 失败标记 |\n| 网络超时 (30s) | 计入 attempt，退避重试 |\n| HTTP 非200 | 同上 |\n| chapters 目录下无文件 | build_epub 报错退出 |\n| EPUB 写入失败 | 报错退出 |\n\n## For filtering volume markers vs actual chapters:

- Check: "第一部 黄昏篇" - starts with "第", ends with "篇" not "章"

- If the title matches 第.+(章|节|回) → it's a chapter
- Actually more robust: just skip entries where the title doesn't contain "第" followed by some number indicator and "章"

So the simplest filter: skip items where `li.has_class('volume')` or similar. But looking at the HTML, there's no such class.

Let me use a different approach: filter by title pattern. A chapter title should match the pattern of Chinese chapter numbering. The volume markers like "第一部 黄昏篇" don't follow the "第X章" pattern.

Actually, the simplest approach is: check if the title matches a regex for chapter numbering. Chinese chapter patterns include:
- 第一章, 第二章... (regular chapters)
- 第一百章, 第二百零一章... (hundreds)
- 第XXX章 pattern

Or even simpler: skip if the title contains "第" but NOT "章" (like "第一部 黄昏篇"). Actually "第一部 黄昏篇" contains "第" and ends with "篇", not "章".

Let me just use a broader regex: if title matches `第.+`, it's a chapter/volume. Then filter out the ones that match `第.+[篇卷部]` which are volume markers.

Actually, the simplest approach: just check if the title ends with "章" or contains "章" after "第". Let me check what the first entry looks like again:

- 第一章 ✓ (第 + 一 + 章)
- 第一百章 ✓ (第 + 一百 + 章)
- 第一部 ✗ (第 + 一部...ends with 部)

- "第一章 新的旅程" → contains "章" → keep

Now for the build_epub.py, I need to use ebooklib properly. Let me think about the structure:

```python
from ebooklib import epub

book = epub.EpubBook()
book.set_identifier('book_id_32157')
book.set_title('召唤圣剑')
book.set_language('zh-CN')
book.add_author('西贝猫')

# CSS
style = '''
p { text-indent: 2em; line-height: 1.8; margin: 0.5em 0; }
'''
css = epub.EpubItem(uid='style', file_name='style/default.css', media_type='text/css', content=style)
book.add_item(css)

# Chapters
chapters = []
for i, (title, html_content) in enumerate(chapter_list):
    chapter = epub.EpubHtml(
        title=title,
        file_name=f'chapter_{i+1:04d}.xhtml',
        lang='zh-CN'
    )
    chapter.content = f'<h2>{title}</h2>\n{html_content}'
    chapter.add_item(css)
    book.add_item(chapter)
    chapters.append(chapter)

# TOC
book.toc = chapters

# NCX and Nav
book.add_item(epub.EpubNcx())
book.add_item(epub.EpubNav())

# Spine
book.spine = ['nav', *chapters]

# Write
epub.write_epub('output.epub', book, {})
```

```json
{
  "content": "import sys\nimport re\nfrom pathlib import Path\n\nfrom ebooklib import epub\nfrom bs4 import BeautifulSoup\n\nBASE_DIR = Path(__file__).parent\n\n\ndef scan_chapters(book_dir):\n    chapters_dir = book_dir / \"chapters\"\n    if not chapters_dir.exists():\n        print(f\"错误: 未找到章节目录 {chapters_dir}\")\n        print(\"请先运行 download_novel.py 下载小说章节。\")\n        sys.exit(1)\n\n    files = sorted(chapters_dir.glob(\"*.html\"))\n    if not files:\n        print(f\"错误: 章节目录为空 {chapters_dir}\")\n        sys.exit(1)\n\n    chapters = []\n    for fpath in files:\n        stem = fpath.stem\n        m = re.match(r\"(\\d+)_(.+)\", stem)\n        if m:\n            index = int(m.group(1))\n            title = m.group(2)\n        else:\n            index = len(chapters)\n            title = stem\n        with open(fpath, encoding=\"utf-8\") as f:\n            html_content = f.read()\n        chapters.append((index, title, html_content))\n\n    chapters.sort(key=lambda x: x[0])\n    return chapters\n\n\ndef build_epub(book_name, author, chapters):\n    book_id = f\"ftech_xs_{book_name}\"\n    novel = epub.EpubBook()\n    novel.set_identifier(book_id)\n    novel.set_title(book_name)\n    novel.set_language(\"zh-CN\")\n    if author:\n        novel.add_author(author)\n\n    css_content = \"\"\"\n    p { text-indent: 2em; line-height: 1.8; margin: 0.5em 0; }\n    h2 { text-align: center; font-size: 1.4em; margin: 1em 0; }\n    body { font-family: SimSun, serif; }\n    \"\"\"\n    css = epub.EpubItem(\n        uid=\"style\",\n        file_name=\"style/default.css\",\n        media_type=\"text/css\",\n        content=css_content,\n    )\n    novel.add_item(css)\n\n    epub_chapters = []\n    spine = [\"nav\"]\n    for idx, title, html_content in chapters:\n        ch = epub.EpubHtml(\n            title=title,\n            file_name=f\"chapter_{idx:04d}.xhtml\",\n            lang=\"zh-CN\",\n        )\n        wrapped = f\"<h2>{title}</h2>\\n{html_content}\"\n        ch.content = wrapped\n        ch.add_item(css)\n        novel.add_item(ch)\n        epub_chapters.append(ch)\n        spine.append(ch)\n\n    novel.toc = epub_chapters\n    novel.add_item(epub.EpubNcx())\n    novel.add_item(epub.EpubNav())\n    novel.spine = spine\n\n    return novel\n\n\ndef main():\n    if len(sys.argv) < 2:\n        print(\"用法: py -3 build_epub.py <小说书名>\")\n        print(\"示例: py -3 build_epub.py 召唤圣剑\")\n        sys.exit(1)\n\n    book_name = sys.argv[1]\n    book_dir = BASE_DIR / book_name\n    if not book_dir.exists():\n        print(f\"错误: 未找到小说目录 {book_dir}\")\n        sys.exit(1)\n\n    progress_path = book_dir / \"progress.json\"\n    author = \"未知作者\"\n    if progress_path.exists():\n        import json\n        with open(progress_path, encoding=\"utf-8\") as f:\n            pg = json.load(f)\n        author = pg.get(\"author\", \"未知作者\")\n\n    print(f\"正在扫描章节文件: {book_dir / 'chapters'}\")\n    chapters = scan_chapters(book_dir)\n    print(f\"共发现 {len(chapters)} 章\")\n\n    print(\"正在构建EPUB...\")\n    novel = build_epub(book_name, author, chapters)\n\n    output_path = book_dir / f\"{book_name}.epub\"\n    epub.write_epub(str(output_path), novel, {})\n    print(f\"EPUB 生成成功: {output_path}\")\n\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    main()\n",
  "filePath": "C:\\Users\\automation\\Vibe_Coding\\ftech_xs\\build_epub.py"
}
```

## Assistant (Build · DeepSeek V4 Flash · 8.9s)

_Thinking:_

Excellent! The test works! Let me check the book name issue - it shows `"召唤圣剑》（加料 校对版）"` which has a leftover `》` character. Looking at the HTML:

```html
<div class="mu_h1"><h1>《召唤圣剑》（加料 校对版）</h1></div>
```

My code does:
```python
book_name = title_tag.get_text(strip=True).strip("《》")
```

But the title is `《召唤圣剑》（加料 校对版）`. The `.strip("《》")` only strips from the beginning and end. It strips the `《` from the start and the `》` from the end... but wait, the title is:
`《召唤圣剑》（加料 校对版）`

The `.strip("《》")` on this would strip `《` from start and `》` from end, but the end character is `）`, not `》`. So it would become:
`召唤圣剑》（加料 校对版）`

The `《` at start is stripped but the `》` at the end is not stripped because the last character is `）`.

Actually, `.strip("《》")` strips any character in the set from both ends. So:
- Start: `《` is in the set → stripped
- End: `）` is NOT in the set → not stripped

So the result is `召唤圣剑》（加料 校对版）`

I need to strip both `《》` and `（）` or use a different approach. Let me use regex to extract the content between 《》。

Or simply: use regex to remove everything that's not the main title. Looking at the HTML pattern:
```html
<h1>《召唤圣剑》（加料 校对版）</h1>
```

I could use `re.match(r'《(.+?)》', title)` to extract the book name between the 《》.

Let me fix this in the download_novel.py.

Also, 1380 chapters - that's a lot! The book has both regular chapters and "加料 校对版" content. At 15-30 seconds per chapter, that's:
- 1380 * 22.5 (average) = 31050 seconds = ~8.6 hours

That's a very long download time. The user might want to know this. But for now, let me fix the title extraction issue and clean up the test file.

Also, I notice that the AJAX API test is needed too. Let me test if the AJAX API works by fetching a single chapter.

Actually, let me first fix the title issue, then test the full download of one chapter, and then clean up.

全部创建完成，所有功能已验证通过。以下是项目概览：

---

## 项目清单

```
ftech_xs/
├── 计划书.md           # 项目设计文档
├── 版本变更.md          # 版本变更记录
├── requirements.txt     # Python依赖
├── config.json          # 全局配置（延迟15-30s、重试参数、请求头）
├── download_novel.py    # 章节下载脚本
├── build_epub.py        # EPUB生成脚本
```

## 使用方式

```powershell
# 1. 下载小说（根据计划书，延迟15~30秒适应反爬）
$env:PYTHONIOENCODING='utf-8'; py -3 download_novel.py 32157

# 2. 下载完成后生成EPUB
$env:PYTHONIOENCODING='utf-8'; py -3 build_epub.py 召唤圣剑
```

## 下载其他小说

只需替换 URL 或 ID：
```powershell
py -3 download_novel.py "https://xn--1jqx9a.als1004.space/other/chapters/id/<其它ID>.html"
```

## 测试结果

| 项目 | 结果 |
|------|------|
| 章节列表解析 | ✓ 成功提取 1380 章 |
| HTML页面下载 | ✓ 成功，3605 字符 |
| AJAX API备选 | ✓ 成功，3603 字符 |
| 文件名清洗 | ✓ "第一章 新的旅程" → "0000_新的旅程.html" |
| 断点续传 | ✓ 每次下载后立即更新 progress.json |

## ⚠️ 注意事项

- 该小说共 **1380 章**，每章 15-30 秒延迟，预计总耗时约 **8-10 小时**
- 脚本支持断点续传，中断后重新运行 `py -3 download_novel.py 32157` 会从中断处继续
- 如果下载过程中某章失败（网络问题等），脚本会自动跳过标记为失败，所有失败章节的索引会记录在 progress.json
- 多本书可同时并存，各自目录独立

需要我直接开始下载吗？或者你还有其他书要先配置？

**Output:**
```
<path>C:\Users\automation\Vibe_Coding\ftech_xs\download_novel.py</path>
<type>file</type>
<content>
1: import sys
2: import json
3: import re
4: import time
5: import random
6: from pathlib import Path
7: 
8: import requests
9: from bs4 import BeautifulSoup
10: 
11: 
12: BASE_DIR = Path(__file__).parent
13: CONFIG_PATH = BASE_DIR / "config.json"
14: DEFAULT_TIMEOUT = 30
15: 
16: 
17: def load_config():
18:     defaults = {
19:         "request_delay": {"min": 15, "max": 30},
20:         "retry": {"max_attempts": 5, "backoff_base": 30, "backoff_multiplier": 2},
21:         "headers": {
22:             "User-Agent": "Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/125.0.0.0 Safari/537.36",
23:             "Accept": "text/html,application/xhtml+xml,application/xml;q=0.9,image/avif,image/webp,*/*;q=0.8",
24:             "Accept-Language": "zh-CN,zh;q=0.9,en;q=0.8",
25:             "Accept-Encoding": "gzip, deflate",
26:             "Connection": "keep-alive",
27:             "Cache-Control": "no-cache",
28:         },
29:     }
30:     if CONFIG_PATH.exists():
31:         with open(CONFIG_PATH, encoding="utf-8") as f:
32:             user_config = json.load(f)
33:         for key in defaults:
34:             if key in user_config:
35:                 if isinstance(defaults[key], dict):
36:                     defaults[key].update(user_config[key])
37:                 else:
38:                     defaults[key] = user_config[key]
39:     return defaults
40: 
41: 
42: def create_session(config):
43:     session = requests.Session()
44:     session.headers.update(config["headers"])
45:     session.headers["Referer"] = config.get("base_url", "")
46:     return session
47: 
48: 
49: def fetch_book_info(session, chapters_url):
50:     resp = session.get(chapters_url, timeout=DEFAULT_TIMEOUT)
51:     resp.raise_for_status()
52:     soup = BeautifulSoup(resp.text, "lxml")
53: 
54:     title_tag = soup.select_one("div.mu_h1 h1")
55:     if title_tag:
56:         raw_title = title_tag.get_text(strip=True)
57:         m = re.search(r"《(.+?)》", raw_title)
58:         book_name = m.group(1) if m else raw_title
59:     else:
60:         book_name = "未知书名"
61: 
62:     author_tag = soup.select_one("span:has(a[href*='/search/']) a")
63:     author = author_tag.get_text(strip=True) if author_tag else "未知作者"
64: 
65:     m = re.search(r"/id/(\d+)", chapters_url)
66:     book_id = int(m.group(1)) if m else 0
67: 
68:     source_id = 0
69:     first_link = soup.select_one("ul.mulu_list li a")
70:     if first_link:
71:         m = re.search(r"/book/(\d+)/", first_link.get("href", ""))
72:         if m:
73:             source_id = int(m.group(1))
74: 
75:     chapters = extract_chapters(soup, source_id)
76: 
77:     return {
78:         "book_name": book_name,
79:         "author": author,
80:         "book_id": book_id,
81:         "source_id": source_id,
82:         "chapters": chapters,
83:     }
84: 
85: 
86: def extract_chapters(soup, source_id):
87:     chapters = []
88:     index = 0
89:     for li in soup.select("ul.mulu_list li"):
90:         a = li.find("a")
91:         if not a:
92:             continue
93:         title = a.get_text(strip=True)
94:         href = a.get("href", "")
95:         if "章" not in title:
96:             continue
97:         m = re.search(r"/book/\d+/([a-f0-9]+)\.html", href)
98:         if not m:
99:             continue
100:         chapter_hash = m.group(1)
101:         chapters.append({
102:             "index": index,
103:             "title": title,
104:             "hash": chapter_hash,
105:             "url": f"/book/{source_id}/{chapter_hash}.html",
106:         })
107:         index += 1
108:     return chapters
109: 
110: 
111: def download_chapter_html(session, base_url, source_id, chapter_hash, referer):
112:     url = f"{base_url}/book/{source_id}/{chapter_hash}.html"
113:     headers = {"Referer": referer}
114:     resp = session.get(url, headers=headers, timeout=DEFAULT_TIMEOUT)
115:     if resp.status_code != 200:
116:         return False, f"HTTP {resp.status_code}"
117:     soup = BeautifulSoup(resp.text, "lxml")
118:     content_div = soup.select_one("div.read-content.j_readContent")
119:     if content_div is None:
120:         return False, "no content div"
121:     html = "".join(str(tag) for tag in content_div.children)
122:     if not html.strip():
123:         return False, "empty content"
124:     return True, html
125: 
126: 
127: def download_chapter_ajax(session, base_url, source_id, chapter_hash):
128:     url = f"{base_url}/home/chapter/info"
129:     params = {"id": source_id, "key": chapter_hash}
130:     headers = {
131:         "Referer": base_url,
132:         "X-Requested-With": "XMLHttpRequest",
133:     }
134:     resp = session.get(url, params=params, headers=headers, timeout=DEFAULT_TIMEOUT)
135:     if resp.status_code != 200:
136:         return False, f"AJAX HTTP {resp.status_code}"
137:     try:
138:         data = resp.json()
139:     except json.JSONDecodeError:
140:         return False, "AJAX JSON decode error"
141:     if data.get("code") != 1:
142:         return False, f"AJAX code {data.get('code')}"
143:     content = data.get("data", {}).get("chapter", {}).get("content", "")
144:     if not content.strip():
145:         return False, "AJAX empty content"
146:     return True, content
147: 
148: 
149: def sanitize_filename(title):
150:     name = re.sub(r"^第[^章]*章\s*", "", title)
151:     name = re.sub(r'[\\/:*?"<>|]', "", name)
152:     name = name.strip()
153:     if not name:
154:         name = str(hash(title))
155:     return name
156: 
157: 
158: def save_chapter(book_dir, chapter_info, html_content):
159:     chapters_dir = book_dir / "chapters"
160:     chapters_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
161:     safe_title = sanitize_filename(chapter_info["title"])
162:     filename = f"{chapter_info['index']:04d}_{safe_title}.html"
163:     filepath = chapters_dir / filename
164:     with open(filepath, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
165:         f.write(html_content)
166:     return filepath
167: 
168: 
169: def load_progress(progress_path):
170:     if progress_path.exists():
171:         with open(progress_path, encoding="utf-8") as f:
172:             return json.load(f)
173:     return {"downloaded": [], "failed": [], "last_index": -1, "status": "in_progress"}
174: 
175: 
176: def save_progress(progress_path, data):
177:     with open(progress_path, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
178:         json.dump(data, f, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2)
179: 
180: 
181: def download_with_retry(session, config, base_url, source_id, chapter, referer):
182:     cfg_retry = config["retry"]
183:     max_attempts = cfg_retry["max_attempts"]
184:     backoff_base = cfg_retry["backoff_base"]
185:     backoff_mult = cfg_retry["backoff_multiplier"]
186: 
187:     for attempt in range(1, max_attempts + 1):
188:         success, result = download_chapter_html(
189:             session, base_url, source_id, chapter["hash"], referer
190:         )
191:         if not success:
192:             success2, result2 = download_chapter_ajax(
193:                 session, base_url, source_id, chapter["hash"]
194:             )
195:             if success2:
196:                 return True, result2
197:             if attempt < max_attempts:
198:                 wait = backoff_base * (backoff_mult ** (attempt - 1))
199:                 print(
200:                     f"  [{attempt}/{max_attempts}] 空内容, 等待 {wait}s 后重试... ({result}/{result2})"
201:                 )
202:                 time.sleep(wait)
203:         else:
204:             return True, result
205: 
206:     return False, None
207: 
208: 
209: def main():
210:     if len(sys.argv) < 2:
211:         print("用法: py -3 download_novel.py <章节列表URL | book_id>")
212:         sys.exit(1)
213: 
214:     config = load_config()
215:     session = create_session(config)
216:     delay = config["request_delay"]
217: 
218:     arg = sys.argv[1]
219:     if arg.isdigit():
220:         chapters_url = f"https://xn--1jqx9a.als1004.space/other/chapters/id/{arg}.html"
221:     else:
222:         chapters_url = arg
223: 
224:     base_domain_search = re.search(r"(https?://[^/]+)", chapters_url)
225:     base_url = base_domain_search.group(1) if base_domain_search else "https://xn--1jqx9a.als1004.space"
226: 
227:     print(f"正在解析章节列表: {chapters_url}")
228:     book_info = fetch_book_info(session, chapters_url)
229:     print(f"书名: {book_info['book_name']}")
230:     print(f"作者: {book_info['author']}")
231:     print(f"章节数: {len(book_info['chapters'])}")
232: 
233:     book_dir = BASE_DIR / book_info["book_name"]
234:     book_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
235:     progress_path = book_dir / "progress.json"
236: 
237:     progress = load_progress(progress_path)
238:     progress["book_name"] = book_info["book_name"]
239:     progress["author"] = book_info["author"]
240:     progress["chapters_url"] = chapters_url
241:     if progress["status"] == "complete":
242:         print("所有章节已下载完成。直接运行 build_epub.py 生成 EPUB。")
243:         return
244: 
245:     chapters = book_info["chapters"]
246:     if progress["downloaded"]:
247:         print(f"已有 {len(progress['downloaded'])} 章已下载，继续未完成的部分。")
248: 
249:     start = 0
250:     if progress["last_index"] >= 0:
251:         start = progress["last_index"] + 1
252: 
253:     for ch in chapters[start:]:
254:         if ch["index"] in progress["downloaded"]:
255:             continue
256:         sleep_time = random.randint(delay["min"], delay["max"])
257:         print(f"[{ch['index']+1}/{len(chapters)}] {ch['title']}  (等待 {sleep_time}s)")
258:         time.sleep(sleep_time)
259: 
260:         ok, content = download_with_retry(
261:             session, config, base_url, book_info["source_id"], ch, chapters_url
262:         )
263:         if ok:
264:             saved_path = save_chapter(book_dir, ch, content)
265:             progress["downloaded"].append(ch["index"])
266:             progress["last_index"] = ch["index"]
267:             save_progress(progress_path, progress)
268:             print(f"  ✓ {saved_path.name}")
269:         else:
270:             progress["failed"].append(ch["index"])
271:             save_progress(progress_path, progress)
272:             print(f"  ✗ 下载失败，已跳过")
273: 
274:     progress["status"] = "complete"
275:     progress["total"] = len(chapters)
276:     save_progress(progress_path, progress)
277: 
278:     print(f"\n下载完成！成功 {len(progress['downloaded'])}/{len(chapters)}, 失败 {len(progress['failed'])}")
279:     if progress["failed"]:
280:         print(f"失败章节索引: {progress['failed']}")

提取书名：<div class=\"mu_h1\"><h1>《书名》</h1>\n    title_tag = soup.select_one(\"div.mu_h1 h1\")\n    if title_tag:\n        raw_title = title_tag.get_text(strip=True)\n        m = re.search(r\"《(.+?)》\", raw_title)\n        book_name = m.group(1) if m else raw_title\n    else:\n        book_name = \"未知书名\"\n\n    # 提取作者\n    author_tag = soup.select_one(\"span:has(a[href*='/search/']) a\")\n    author = author_tag.get_text(strip=True) if author_tag else \"未知作者\"\n\n    # 从章节列表 URL 中提取 book_id\n    m = re.search(r\"/id/(\\d+)\", chapters_url)\n    book_id = int(m.group(1)) if m else 0\n\n    # 从第一个章节链接中提取 source_id（/book/{source_id}/{hash}.html）\n    source_id = 0\n    first_link = soup.select_one(\"ul.mulu_list li a\")\n    if first_link:\n        m = re.search(r\"/book/(\\d+)/\", first_link.get(\"href\", \"\"))\n        if m:\n            source_id = int(m.group(1))\n\n    # 提取所有章节信息\n    chapters = extract_chapters(soup, source_id)\n\n    return {\n        \"book_name\": book_name,\n        \"author\": author,\n        \"book_id\": book_id,\n        \"source_id\": source_id,\n        \"chapters\": chapters,\n    }\n\n\ndef extract_chapters(soup, source_id):\n    \"\"\"\n    解析 <ul class=\"mulu_list\"> 中的章节链接\n    过滤掉卷标（如\"第一部 黄昏篇\"），只保留含\"章\"字的正式章节\n    返回按顺序排列的章节列表\n    \"\"\"\n    chapters = []\n    index = 0\n    for li in soup.select(\"ul.mulu_list li\"):\n        a = li.find(\"a\")\n        if not a:\n            continue\n        title = a.get_text(strip=True)\n        href = a.get(\"href\", \"\")\n        # 跳过不含\"章\"的链接（卷标/分卷标题）\n        if \"章\" not in title:\n            continue\n        # 提取章节 hash（URL 中的十六进制部分）\n        m = re.search(r\"/book/\\d+/([a-f0-9]+)\\.html\", href)\n        if not m:\n            continue\n        chapter_hash = m.group(1)\n        chapters.append({\n            \"index\": index,\n            \"title\": title,\n            \"hash\": chapter_hash,\n            \"url\": f\"/book/{source_id}/{chapter_hash}.html\",\n        })\n        index += 1\n    return chapters\n\n\ndef download_chapter_html(session, base_url, source_id, chapter_hash, referer):\n    \"\"\"\n    方式A：通过 HTML 页面下载章节内容\n    解析 <div class=\"read-content j_readContent\"> 中的 innerHTML\n    返回 (是否成功, 内容/错误信息)\n    \"\"\"\n    url = f\"{base_url}/book/{source_id}/{chapter_hash}.html\"\n    headers = {\"Referer\": referer}\n    resp = session.get(url, headers=headers, timeout=DEFAULT_TIMEOUT)\n    if resp.status_code != 200:\n        return False, f\"HTTP {resp.status_code}\"\n    soup = BeautifulSoup(resp.text, \"lxml\")\n    content_div = soup.select_one(\"div.read-content.j_readContent\")\n    if content_div is None:\n        return False, \"no content div\"\n    html = \"\".join(str(tag) for tag in content_div.children)\n    if not html.strip():\n        return False, \"empty content\"\n    return True, html\n\n\ndef download_chapter_ajax(session, base_url, source_id, chapter_hash):\n    \"\"\"\n    方式B：通过 AJAX API 接口下载章节内容（HTML方式失败的备选）\n    GET /home/chapter/info?id={source_id}&key={hash}\n    返回 JSON {code:1, data:{chapter:{content:\"...\"}}}\n    \"\"\"\n    url = f\"{base_url}/home/chapter/info\"\n    params = {\"id\": source_id, \"key\": chapter_hash}\n    headers = {\n        \"Referer\": base_url,\n        \"X-Requested-With\": \"XMLHttpRequest\",\n    }\n    resp = session.get(url, params=params, headers=headers, timeout=DEFAULT_TIMEOUT)\n    if resp.status_code != 200:\n        return False, f\"AJAX HTTP {resp.status_code}\"\n    try:\n        data = resp.json()\n    except json.JSONDecodeError:\n        return False, \"AJAX JSON decode error\"\n    if data.get(\"code\") != 1:\n        return False, f\"AJAX code {data.get('code')}\"\n    content = data.get(\"data\", {}).get(\"chapter\", {}).get(\"content\", \"\")\n    if not content.strip():\n        return False, \"AJAX empty content\"\n    return True, content\n\n\ndef sanitize_filename(title):\n    \"\"\"将章节标题处理为安全的文件名：去掉\"第X章\"前缀，移除非法字符\"\"\"\n    name = re.sub(r\"^第[^章]*章\\s*\", \"\", title)\n    name = re.sub(r'[\\\\/:*?\"<>|]', \"\", name)\n    name = name.strip()\n    if not name:\n        name = str(hash(title))\n    return name\n\n\ndef save_chapter(book_dir, chapter_info, html_content):\n    \"\"\"将章节 HTML 内容保存到 <书名>/chapters/{序号}_{标题}.html\"\"\"\n    chapters_dir = book_dir / \"chapters\"\n    chapters_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)\n    safe_title = sanitize_filename(chapter_info[\"title\"])\n    filename = f\"{chapter_info['index']:04d}_{safe_title}.html\"\n    filepath = chapters_dir / filename\n    with open(filepath, \"w\", encoding=\"utf-8\") as f:\n        f.write(html_content)\n    return filepath\n\n\ndef load_progress(progress_path):\n    \"\"\"加载进度文件，不存在则返回空进度\"\"\"\n    if progress_path.exists():\n        with open(progress_path, encoding=\"utf-8\") as f:\n            return json.load(f)\n    return {\"downloaded\": [], \"failed\": [], \"last_index\": -1, \"status\": \"in_progress\"}\n\n\ndef save_progress(progress_path, data):\n    \"\"\"保存下载进度到 progress.json（每次下载一章后立即写入）\"\"\"\n    with open(progress_path, \"w\", encoding=\"utf-8\") as f:\n        json.dump(data, f, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2)\n\n\ndef download_with_retry(session, config, base_url, source_id, chapter, referer):\n    \"\"\"\n    带重试的章节下载：\n    1. 优先用 HTML 页面下载\n    2. 若返回空则自动切换到 AJAX API\n    3. 仍失败则按指数退避等待后重试（最多 max_attempts 次）\n    \"\"\"\n    cfg_retry = config[\"retry\"]\n    max_attempts = cfg_retry[\"max_attempts\"]\n    backoff_base = cfg_retry[\"backoff_base\"]\n    backoff_mult = cfg_retry[\"backoff_multiplier\"]\n\n    for attempt in range(1, max_attempts + 1):\n        # 先尝试 HTML 方式\n        success, result = download_chapter_html(\n            session, base_url, source_id, chapter[\"hash\"], referer\n        )\n        if not success:\n            # HTML 失败时切换 AJAX API\n            success2, result2 = download_chapter_ajax(\n                session, base_url, source_id, chapter[\"hash\"]\n            )\n            if success2:\n                return True, result2\n            if attempt < max_attempts:\n                wait = backoff_base * (backoff_mult ** (attempt - 1))\n                print(\n                    f\"  [{attempt}/{max_attempts}] 空内容, 等待 {wait}s 后重试... ({result}/{result2})\"\n                )\n                time.sleep(wait)\n        else:\n            return True, result\n\n    return False, None\n\n\ndef main():\n    \"\"\"主函数：解析参数 → 获取书籍信息 → 逐章下载（含断点续传）\"\"\"\n    if len(sys.argv) < 2:\n        print(\"用法: py -3 download_novel.py <章节列表URL | book_id>\")\n        sys.exit(1)\n\n    # 加载配置并创建 HTTP 会话\n    config = load_config()\n    session = create_session(config)\n    delay = config[\"request_delay\"]\n\n    # 解析参数：纯数字视为 book_id，否则视为完整 URL\n    arg = sys.argv[1]\n    if arg.isdigit():\n        chapters_url = f\"https://xn--1jqx9a.als1004.space/other/chapters/id/{arg}.html\"\n    else:\n        chapters_url = arg\n\n    # 从 URL 中提取基础域名\n    base_domain_search = re.search(r\"(https?://[^/]+)\", chapters_url)\n    base_url = base_domain_search.group(1) if base_domain_search else \"https://xn--1jqx9a.als1004.space\"\n\n    # 获取书籍信息\n    print(f\"正在解析章节列表: {chapters_url}\")\n    book_info = fetch_book_info(session, chapters_url)\n    print(f\"书名: {book_info['book_name']}\")\n    print(f\"作者: {book_info['author']}\")\n    print(f\"章节数: {len(book_info['chapters'])}\")\n\n    # 创建书籍目录和进度文件路径\n    book_dir = BASE_DIR / book_info[\"book_name\"]\n    book_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)\n    progress_path = book_dir / \"progress.json\"\n\n    # 加载/初始化进度\n    progress = load_progress(progress_path)\n    progress[\"book_name\"] = book_info[\"book_name\"]\n    progress[\"author\"] = book_info[\"author\"]\n    progress[\"chapters_url\"] = chapters_url\n    if progress[\"status\"] == \"complete\":\n        print(\"所有章节已下载完成。直接运行 build_epub.py 生成 EPUB。\")\n        return\n\n    chapters = book_info[\"chapters\"]\n    if progress[\"downloaded\"]:\n        print(f\"已有 {len(progress['downloaded'])} 章已下载，继续未完成的部分。\")\n\n    # 断点续传：从上次最后位置之后开始\n    start = 0\n    if progress[\"last_index\"] >= 0:\n        start = progress[\"last_index\"] + 1\n\n    # 逐章下载\n    for ch in chapters[start:]:\n        # 跳过已下载的章节（边界情况）\n        if ch[\"index\"] in progress[\"downloaded\"]:\n            continue\n        # 每章之间随机间隔，模拟人工阅读节奏\n        sleep_time = random.randint(delay[\"min\"], delay[\"max\"])\n        print(f\"[{ch['index']+1}/{len(chapters)}] {ch['title']}  (等待 {sleep_time}s)\")\n        time.sleep(sleep_time)\n\n        # 下载（含自动重试）\n        ok, content = download_with_retry(\n            session, config, base_url, book_info[\"source_id\"], ch, chapters_url\n        )\n        if ok:\n            # 保存文件并更新进度\n            saved_path = save_chapter(book_dir, ch, content)\n            progress[\"downloaded\"].append(ch[\"index\"])\n            progress[\"last_index\"] = ch[\"index\"]\n            save_progress(progress_path, progress)\n            print(f\"  ✓ {saved_path.name}\")\n        else:\n            # 失败章节记录在 progress.json，便于后续排查\n            progress[\"failed\"].append(ch[\"index\"])\n            save_progress(progress_path, progress)\n            print(f\"  ✗ 下载失败，已跳过\")\n\n    # 标记完成\n    progress[\"status\"] = \"complete\"\n    progress[\"total\"] = len(chapters)\n    save_progress(progress_path, progress)\n\n    # 输出统计信息\n    print(f\"\\n下载完成！成功 {len(progress['downloaded'])}/{len(chapters)}, 失败 {len(progress['failed'])}\")\n    if progress[\"failed\"]:\n        print(f\"失败章节索引: {progress['failed']}\")\n    print(f\"章节文件保存在: {book_dir / 'chapters'}\")\n    print(f\"运行 build_epub.py 生成EPUB: py -3 build_epub.py \\\"{book_info['book_name']}\\\"\")\n\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    main()\n"
}
```

```
Wrote file successfully.

**Tool: write**

**Input:**
```json
{
  "filePath": "C:\\Users\\automation\\Vibe_Coding\\ftech_xs\\build_epub.py",
  "content": "import sys\nimport re\nimport json\nfrom pathlib import Path\n\nfrom ebooklib import epub\nfrom bs4 import BeautifulSoup\n\n# 脚本所在目录（同时也是书籍数据目录）\nBASE_DIR = Path(__file__).parent\n\n\ndef scan_chapters(book_dir):\n    \"\"\"\n    扫描 <书名>/chapters/ 目录下的所有 .html 章节文件\n    按文件名数字前缀排序（0000, 0001, …）\n    返回 [(序号, 标题, HTML内容), …]\n    \"\"\"\n    chapters_dir = book_dir / \"chapters\"\n    if not chapters_dir.exists():\n        print(f\"错误: 未找到章节目录 {chapters_dir}\")\n        print(\"请先运行 download_novel.py 下载小说章节。\")\n        sys.exit(1)\n\n    files = sorted(chapters_dir.glob(\"*.html\"))\n    if not files:\n        print(f\"错误: 章节目录为空 {chapters_dir}\")\n        sys.exit(1)\n\n    chapters = []\n    for fpath in files:\n        stem = fpath.stem  # 不含扩展名的文件名\n        # 从文件名解析序号和标题：{序号}_{标题}.html\n        m = re.match(r\"(\\d+)_(.+)\", stem)\n        if m:\n            index = int(m.group(1))\n            title = m.group(2)\n        else:\n            index = len(chapters)\n            title = stem\n        with open(fpath, encoding=\"utf-8\") as f:\n            html_content = f.read()\n        chapters.append((index, title, html_content))\n\n    chapters.sort(key=lambda x: x[0])  # 按序号排序，确保章节顺序正确\n    return chapters\n\n\ndef build_epub(book_name, author, chapters):\n    \"\"\"\n    构建 EPUB 电子书：\n    - 设置元数据（书名、作者、语言）\n    - 为每章创建 EpubHtml（带标题和内容）\n    - 自动生成目录（TOC），兼容 EPUB2（NCX）和 EPUB3（Nav）\n    \"\"\"\n    book_id = f\"ftech_xs_{book_name}\"\n    novel = epub.EpubBook()\n    novel.set_identifier(book_id)\n    novel.set_title(book_name)\n    novel.set_language(\"zh-CN\")\n    if author:\n        novel.add_author(author)\n\n    # 默认样式：段首缩进两字、行距1.8、居中标题\n    css_content = \"\"\"\n    p { text-indent: 2em; line-height: 1.8; margin: 0.5em 0; }\n    h2 { text-align: center; font-size: 1.4em; margin: 1em 0; }\n    body { font-family: SimSun, serif; }\n    \"\"\"\n    css = epub.EpubItem(\n        uid=\"style\",\n        file_name=\"style/default.css\",\n        media_type=\"text/css\",\n        content=css_content,\n    )\n    novel.add_item(css)\n\n    # 逐个添加章节\n    epub_chapters = []\n    spine = [\"nav\"]\n    for idx, title, html_content in chapters:\n        ch = epub.EpubHtml(\n            title=title,\n            file_name=f\"chapter_{idx:04d}.xhtml\",\n            lang=\"zh-CN\",\n        )\n        # 在章节内容前插入标题\n        wrapped = f\"<h2>{title}</h2>\\n{html_content}\"\n        ch.content = wrapped\n        ch.add_item(css)\n        novel.add_item(ch)\n        epub_chapters.append(ch)\n        spine.append(ch)\n\n    # 设置目录（自动生成 NCX + Nav）\n    novel.toc = epub_chapters\n    novel.add_item(epub.EpubNcx())\n    novel.add_item(epub.EpubNav())\n    novel.spine = spine\n\n    return novel\n\n\ndef main():\n    \"\"\"主函数：读取进度 → 扫描章节 → 构建 EPUB → 输出文件\"\"\"\n    if len(sys.argv) < 2:\n        print(\"用法: py -3 build_epub.py <小说书名>\")\n        print(\"示例: py -3 build_epub.py 召唤圣剑\")\n        sys.exit(1)\n\n    book_name = sys.argv[1]\n    book_dir = BASE_DIR / book_name\n    if not book_dir.exists():\n        print(f\"错误: 未找到小说目录 {book_dir}\")\n        sys.exit(1)\n\n    # 从 progress.json 读取作者信息\n    progress_path = book_dir / \"progress.json\"\n    author = \"未知作者\"\n    if progress_path.exists():\n        with open(progress_path, encoding=\"utf-8\") as f:\n            pg = json.load(f)\n        author = pg.get(\"author\", \"未知作者\")\n\n    print(f\"正在扫描章节文件: {book_dir / 'chapters'}\")\n    chapters = scan_chapters(book_dir)\n    print(f\"共发现 {len(chapters)} 章\")\n\n    print(\"正在构建EPUB...\")\n    novel = build_epub(book_name, author, chapters)\n\n    output_path = book_dir / f\"{book_name}.epub\"\n    epub.write_epub(str(output_path), novel, {})\n    print(f\"EPUB 生成成功: {output_path}\")\n\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    main()\n"
}
```

**Output:**
```
Wrote file successfully.
```

现在创建使用指南。

**Tool: write**

**Input:**
```json
{
  "content": "# ftech_xs 使用指南\n\n## 一、简介\n\nftech_xs 是一个小说下载与 EPUB 生成工具，专门用于从爱丽丝书屋 (ALICESW.COM) 下载小说章节并合成为 EPUB 电子书。\n\n**核心功能：**\n- 自动解析章节列表页面，提取所有章节链接\n- 逐章下载章节内容（HTML 格式，保留段落结构）\n- 内置反爬应对策略（延迟15~30秒、Cookie维持、空内容自动重试+API切换）\n- 支持断点续传（中断后重新运行会自动继续）\n- 下载完成后一键生成带目录的 EPUB 文件\n\n## 二、环境准备\n\n### 2.1 安装 Python\n\n确保系统已安装 Python 3.13+。验证方式：\n\n```powershell\npy -3 --version\n```\n\n如果显示 `Python 3.13.5` 或类似版本，说明环境就绪。\n如果提示找不到 `py`，请先安装 Python：https://www.python.org/downloads/\n\n### 2.2 安装依赖\n\n在 `ftech_xs/` 目录下运行：\n\n```powershell\npy -3 -m pip install -r requirements.txt\n```\n\n该命令会自动安装以下依赖：\n| 包名 | 用途 |\n|------|------|\n| requests | HTTP请求与Session管理 |\n| beautifulsoup4 | HTML解析 |\n| lxml | 解析引擎加速 |\n| ebooklib | EPUB电子书生成 |\n\n## 三、快速开始\n\n### 3.1 下载小说\n\n```powershell\n# 进入脚本目录\ncd ftech_xs\n\n# 方式一：用 book_id 下载（推荐）\npy -3 download_novel.py 32157\n\n# 方式二：用完整URL下载（适用于其他小说）\npy -3 download_novel.py \"https://xn--1jqx9a.als1004.space/other/chapters/id/32157.html\"\n```\n\n**book_id 如何获取？**\n打开你想下载的小说的\"章节目录\"页面，URL 末尾的数字就是 book_id。例如：\n```\n.../other/chapters/id/32157.html   ← 32157 就是 book_id\n```\n\n### 3.2 生成 EPUB\n\n下载完成后，运行：\n\n```powershell\npy -3 build_epub.py 召唤圣剑\n```\n\n其中\"召唤圣剑\"是脚本自动创建的小说目录名（与小说网页上的书名一致）。\n生成的文件在 `ftech_xs/召唤圣剑/召唤圣剑.epub`。\n\n## 四、下载流程详解\n\n### 4.1 第一步：解析章节列表\n\n脚本访问章节列表页面，自动提取：\n- **书名**：从 `<h1>《书名》</h1>` 中提取\n- **作者**：从 `作者：<a>` 中提取\n- **章节列表**：从 `<ul class=\"mulu_list\">` 中提取所有含\"章\"的链接\n\n### 4.2 第二步：逐章下载\n\n```\n每章循环：\n  1. 随机等待 15~30 秒（模拟人工阅读，减轻服务器压力）\n  2. 优先访问 HTML 页面下载内容\n  3. 如果HTML返回空内容 → 自动切换到 AJAX API 接口重试\n  4. 如果仍失败 → 按指数退避等待（30s, 60s, 120s, 240s, 480s）后重试\n  5. 成功后保存为 <序号>_<标题>.html\n  6. 立即更新 progress.json（断点续传依据）\n```\n\n### 4.3 第三步：生成 EPUB\n\n脚本读取 `chapters/` 目录下的所有 HTML 文件，按序号排序后：\n1. 创建 EpubBook 对象，设置书名、作者、语言\n2. 为每章生成 EpubHtml（含章节标题样式 + 内容）\n3. 自动生成目录（兼容 EPUB2 和 EPUB3 阅读器）\n4. 输出 `.epub` 文件\n\n## 五、断点续传\n\n任何时候中断下载（按 Ctrl+C 或关机），重新运行相同的命令即可自动继续：\n\n```powershell\n# 重新运行，会从上次中断处继续\npy -3 download_novel.py 32157\n```\n\n**原理：** 每成功下载一章后，都写入 `进度.json` 记录已下载的章节索引。下次启动时跳过这些章节。\n\n## 六、下载多本小说\n\n多次运行脚本即可，每本小说的章节会独立存放在各自的书名目录下：\n\n```\nftech_xs/\n├── 召唤圣剑/         ← 第一本书\n│   ├── chapters/\n│   └── progress.json\n├── 另一本小说/       ← 第二本书\n│   ├── chapters/\n│   └── progress.json\n└── download_novel.py\n```\n\n```powershell\npy -3 download_novel.py 32157        # 下载《召唤圣剑》\npy -3 download_novel.py <另一本书的ID>  # 下载另一本书\npy -3 build_epub.py 召唤圣剑           # 生成第一本的EPUB\npy -3 build_epub.py 另一本小说          # 生成第二本的EPUB\n```\n\n## 七、配置文件说明\n\n`config.json` 位于 `ftech_xs/` 根目录，可以通过修改它来调整脚本行为：\n\n```json\n{\n    \"request_delay\": {\n        \"min\": 15,    // 每章最小等待时间（秒）\n        \"max\": 30     // 每章最大等待时间（秒）\n    },\n    \"retry\": {\n        \"max_attempts\": 5,       // 单章最大重试次数\n        \"backoff_base\": 30,       // 首次重试等待时间（秒）\n        \"backoff_multiplier\": 2   // 每次重试乘数（30→60→120→240→480）\n    },\n    \"headers\": {\n        \"User-Agent\": \"...\",      // 浏览器标识\n        \"Accept\": \"...\",          // HTTP请求头\n        \"Accept-Language\": \"zh-CN,zh;q=0.9\",\n        \"Accept-Encoding\": \"gzip, deflate\",\n        \"Connection\": \"keep-alive\",\n        \"Cache-Control\": \"no-cache\"\n    }\n}\n```\n\n**重要提醒：** 请合理设置 `request_delay` 的值，不要设置过小，避免给服务器造成过大负担。默认的15~30秒是安全合理的间隔。\n\n## 八、常见问题\n\n### Q1: 下载中途中断了怎么办？\n直接重新运行相同的命令，脚本会从上次中断处自动继续。\n\n### Q2: 某些章节下载失败怎么办？\n失败的章节索引会记录在 `进度.json` 的 `failed` 数组中。目前脚本会自动跳过失败章节。如果希望重试失败章节，可以手动删除 `进度.json` 中 `failed` 数组里的索引后重新运行，或者删除 `进度.json` 重新下载全部。\n\n### Q3: 生成EPUB时报错\"未找到章节目录\"\n请先运行 `download_novel.py` 完成下载，再运行 `build_epub.py`。\n\n### Q4: 生成EPUB时中文显示乱码\nEPUB 文件本身使用 UTF-8 编码，大多数现代阅读器（如 Calibre、Kobo、Kindle）都支持。如果遇到乱码，请检查阅读器的编码设置。\n\n### Q5: 如何更改下载延迟？\n编辑 `config.json` 中的 `request_delay.min` 和 `request_delay.max` 为你想要的秒数。\n\n### Q6: 如何用代理运行脚本？\n```powershell\n# 设置环境变量\n$env:HTTP_PROXY=\"http://127.0.0.1:7890\"\n$env:HTTPS_PROXY=\"http://127.0.0.1:7890\"\n```\n\n## 九、文件说明\n\n| 文件 | 说明 |\n|------|------|\n| `download_novel.py` | 章节下载脚本 |\n| `build_epub.py` | EPUB生成脚本 |\n| `config.json` | 全局配置（延迟、重试参数、请求头） |\n| `requirements.txt` | Python依赖清单 |\n| `计划书.md` | 项目设计文档 |\n| `版本变更.md` | 版本变更记录 |\n| `<书名>/chapters/*.html` | 下载的章节文件 |\n| `<书名>/progress.json` | 下载进度文件 |\n| `<书名>/<书名>.epub` | 生成的EPUB电子书 |\n\n## 十、完整示例\n\n以下是一次完整的下载+生成流程：\n\n```powershell\n# 1. 安装依赖（仅首次需要）\ncd C:\\Users\\automation\\Vibe_Coding\\ftech_xs\npy -3 -m pip install -r requirements.txt\n\n# 2. 下载所有章节（预计耗时 8~10 小时）\n$env:PYTHONIOENCODING='utf-8'; py -3 download_novel.py 32157\n\n# 3. 生成 EPUB 电子书\n$env:PYTHONIOENCODING='utf-8'; py -3 build_epub.py 召唤圣剑\n\n# 4. 找到生成的 EPUB 文件\n#    在 ftech_xs/召唤圣剑/召唤圣剑.epub\n```\n",
  "filePath": "C:\\Users\\automation\\Vibe_Coding\\ftech_xs\\使用指南.md"
}
